--RA_sequence.sql
-- 위험요소시퀀스
CREATE SEQUENCE SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR_SEQ  MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 1 NOCACHE  NOORDER  NOCYCLE  NOKEEP  NOSCALE  GLOBAL;

-- 위험평가기준관리(국가)
CREATE SEQUENCE SSQ.RA_ITEM_NTN_SEQ  MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 1 NOCACHE  NOORDER  NOCYCLE  NOKEEP  NOSCALE  GLOBAL;

-- 위험평가기준관리(직업)
CREATE SEQUENCE SSQ.RA_ITEM_IDJOB_SEQ  MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 1 NOCACHE  NOORDER  NOCYCLE  NOKEEP  NOSCALE  GLOBAL;

-- 위험평가기준관리(업종)
CREATE SEQUENCE SSQ.RA_ITEM_CORJOB_SEQ  MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 1 NOCACHE  NOORDER  NOCYCLE  NOKEEP  NOSCALE  GLOBAL;

-- 위험평가기준관리(공통)
CREATE SEQUENCE SSQ.RA_ITEM_COMMON_SEQ  MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 1 NOCACHE  NOORDER  NOCYCLE  NOKEEP  NOSCALE  GLOBAL;

-- 구간관리
CREATE SEQUENCE SSQ.RA_ITEM_STD_REQ  MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 1 NOCACHE  NOORDER  NOCYCLE  NOKEEP  NOSCALE  GLOBAL;
CREATE SEQUENCE SSQ.RA_GRD_STD_REQ  MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 1 NOCACHE  NOORDER  NOCYCLE  NOKEEP  NOSCALE  GLOBAL;

-- 가중치관리
CREATE SEQUENCE SSQ.RA_ITEM_WGHT_SEQ  MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 9999999999 INCREMENT BY 1 START WITH 1 NOCACHE  NOORDER  NOCYCLE  NOKEEP  NOSCALE  GLOBAL;

-- 신상품관련시퀀스
CREATE SEQUENCE SSQ.KYC_PRD_CK_SEQ INCREMENT BY 1 MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 1000000000000000000000000000 NOCYCLE NOCACHE NOORDER;
CREATE SEQUENCE SSQ.KYC_PRD_EVLTN_SEQ INCREMENT BY 1 MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 1000000000000000000000000000 NOCYCLE NOCACHE NOORDER;
CREATE SEQUENCE SSQ.KYC_PRD_EVLTN_ATTACH_SEQ INCREMENT BY 1 MINVALUE 1 MAXVALUE 1000000000000000000000000000 NOCYCLE NOCACHE NOORDER;

--RA_table_script.sql
-- RA_RISK_FACTOR
CREATE TABLE SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR
(
    RISK_CATG1_C        VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
    RISK_CATG2_C        VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
    RISK_ELMT_C         VARCHAR2(10) NOT NULL,
    RISK_ELMT_NM        VARCHAR2(400) NOT NULL,
    RISK_INDI           VARCHAR2(1),
    RISK_CORP           VARCHAR2(1),
    RISK_VAL_ITEM       VARCHAR2(100),
    RISK_VAL_CAL_STD    VARCHAR2(100),
    RISK_APPL_YN        VARCHAR2(1),
    RISK_APPL_MODEL_I   VARCHAR2(1),
    RISK_APPL_MODEL_B   VARCHAR2(1),
    RISK_HRSK_YN        VARCHAR2(1),
    RISK_SCR            NUMBER(6,4),
    RISK_RSN_DESC       VARCHAR2(4000),
    RISK_RMRK           VARCHAR2(4000),
    RISK_REG_DT         DATE,
    RISK_REG_ID         NUMBER,
    RISK_UPD_DT         DATE,
    RISK_UPD_ID         NUMBER
)
TABLESPACE TS_SSQ_DN01
STORAGE
(
    INITIAL 64K
    NEXT 1M
)
NOCOMPRESS;

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX SSQ.PK_RA_RISK_FACTOR
ON SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR (RISK_CATG1_C,RISK_CATG2_C,RISK_ELMT_C) 
TABLESPACE TS_SSQ_DN01
STORAGE
(
    INITIAL 64K
    NEXT 1M
);

ALTER TABLE SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR
ADD CONSTRAINT PK_RA_RISK_FACTOR PRIMARY KEY (RISK_CATG1_C,RISK_CATG2_C,RISK_ELMT_C);

GRANT DELETE ON SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR TO RA_SSQ;
GRANT INSERT ON SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR TO RA_SSQ;
GRANT UPDATE ON SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR TO RA_SSQ;
GRANT SELECT ON SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR TO RA_SSQ;
GRANT SELECT ON SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR TO RS_SSQ;

COMMENT ON TABLE SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR IS '위험요소관리_최종';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_CATG1_C IS '위험분류Lv1';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_CATG2_C IS '위험분류Lv2';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_ELMT_C IS '위험요소코드';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_ELMT_NM IS '위험요소명';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_INDI IS '적용대상(개인/개인사업자)';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_CORP IS '적용대상(법인)';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_VAL_ITEM IS '평가항목';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_VAL_CAL_STD IS '평가기준';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_APPL_YN IS '적용여부';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_APPL_MODEL_I IS '적용모델(I)';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_APPL_MODEL_B IS '적용모델(B)';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_HRSK_YN IS '당연EDD여부';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_SCR IS '위험점수';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_RSN_DESC IS '위험사유';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_RMRK IS '비고';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_REG_DT IS '등록일자';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_REG_ID IS '등록자ID';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_UPD_DT IS '수정일자';
COMMENT ON COLUMN SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR.RISK_UPD_ID IS '수정자ID';

CREATE SYNONYM JSQ0APP.RA_RISK_FACTOR
FOR SSQ.RA_RISK_FACTOR;

    REG_DT          DATE,

    TICPI_CPI_IDX       NUMBER(4,2),
    TICPI_CPI_IDX_SCR   NUMBER(4,2),
    INCRS_PROD_STA      VARCHAR2(10),
    INCRS_PROD_YN       VARCHAR2(1),
    INCRS_CHEM_STA      VARCHAR2(10),
    INCRS_CHEM_YN       VARCHAR2(1),
    BASEL_RIK_STA       NUMBER,
    BASEL_RIK_IDX       NUMBER(4,2),

    HNDL_DY_TM          DATE,
    HNDL_P_ENO          NUMBER
)

(
